120)  1) "summary"
      2) "Creates a key from the serialized representation of a value."
      3) "since"
      4) "2.6.0"
      5) "group"
      6) "generic"
      7) "complexity"
      8) "O(1) to create the new key and additional O(N*M) to reconstruct the serialized value, where N is the number of Redis objects composing the value and M their average size. For small string values the time complexity is thus O(1)+O(1*M) where M is small, so simply O(1). However for sorted set values the complexity is O(N*M*log(N)) because inserting values into sorted sets is O(log(N))."
